#ELECTION DECISION
GRE_1936_election_category = { 
	GRE_the_election_of_1936  = { # Election crisis

		icon = eng_support_imperialist_coup

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
			date > 1936.01.26
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 26

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_1936_election }
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_1936_election }
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			#hidden_effect = { 
                country_event = { id = hellenic_news.1 days = 7 }
				set_country_flag = GRE_1936_election
                complete_national_focus = GRE_election_1936
			#}
		}
	}

	GRE_the_election_of_1936_cont  = { # Election crisis

		icon = eng_support_imperialist_coup

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
			date > 1936.03.5
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 37

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_1936_election_cont }
            has_country_flag = GRE_1936_election
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_1936_election_cont }
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { 
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_country_flag = GRE_king_arrested
					}	
					country_event = { id = bftb_greece.2 days = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = hellenic_news.2 days = 7 }
				}
				set_country_flag = GRE_1936_election_cont
                complete_national_focus = GRE_georges_dictat
                set_country_flag = GRE_faction_gui_flag
			}
		}
	}

	GRE_demertzis_death  = { # Election crisis

		icon = eng_support_imperialist_coup
        on_map_mode = map_only
        highlight_states = { state = -1 }

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
			has_completed_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 102

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
		}

		visible = {
			is_debug = yes
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { 
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_1936_election_tt
			hidden_effect = { 
                country_event = { id = hellenic_news.3 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	GRE_metaxas_vote_of_confidence_hidden  = { # Election crisis

		icon = eng_support_imperialist_coup
        on_map_mode = map_only
        highlight_states = { state = -1 }

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
			has_completed_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 115

			is_debug = yes
		}

	GRE_hidden_strikes_misson  = { # Election crisis

			is_debug = yes
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { 
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_1936_election_tt
			hidden_effect = { 
                country_event = { id = hellenic_news.5 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
    
	GRE_the_election_of_1936_cont_2  = { # Election crisis

		icon = eng_support_imperialist_coup

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
			has_completed_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 8

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
			has_country_flag = GRE_strikes_started
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = GRE_strikes_started
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { 
				set_country_flag = GRE_strikes_dealt
                clr_country_flag = GRE_strikes_started
                country_event = { id = hellas.1 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_1936_election_tt
			hidden_effect = { 
                add_to_variable = { fct_mon = 5}   
                subtract_from_variable = { fct_com = 15}
                subtract_from_variable = { fct_dem = 15}
                add_to_variable = { fct_fas = 2.5}
                faction_gui_call = yes 
                complete_national_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes
			}
		}
	}

}

    GRE_expand_collapse_foreign_manufacturer_buffs = {
        icon = decision_generic_decision
    
        allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}
        
        fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 0
        days_re_enable = 0
        priority = 12
        
        visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
        }
        
        complete_effect = {
            hidden_effect = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_fm }
                    }
                    set_country_flag = toggle_fm
                }
                else = {
                    clr_country_flag = toggle_fm 
                }
            }
        }
    }

    GRE_expand_collapse_low_risk_investments = {
        icon = decision_generic_decision
    
        allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}
        
        fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 0
        days_re_enable = 0
        priority = 10
        
        visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
        }
        
        complete_effect = {
            hidden_effect = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_low_risk }
                    }
                    set_country_flag = toggle_low_risk
                }
                else = {
                    clr_country_flag = toggle_low_risk 
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    GRE_low_risk_investment = {
        icon = generic_factory

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}
        
        priority = 9

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                is_in_array = {
                    array = global.favor_mechanic
                    value = THIS.id
                }          
			}
		}

		available = {
			date < 1942.1.1
            FROM = { exists = yes }
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = GRE_favor_abysmal_from_tt
                    check_variable = { var = FROM.favor@GRE value = 0 compare = less_than }
                }
			}
		}
        
		visible = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_low_risk }
			has_completed_focus = GRE_open_up_the_country
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = {
                        is_major = no
                    }
                }
                check_variable = { var = FROM.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
		}

		modifier = {
            political_power_factor = -0.1
        }
        
        days_remove = 14
        cost = 75

		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = hellas.500 days = 1 }
			}
		}
    }

    GRE_buy_subs_dec = {
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { state = FROM.capital } 

		icon = sub

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = GRE_favor_at_least_mediocre_from_tt
                check_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE > 29 }
            }
            NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                OR = {
                    original_tag = ENG
                    original_tag = GER
                }
			}
		}

		cost = 0
        days_remove = 730

		fire_only_once = no

		visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_buy_subs
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
            NOT = { 
                has_country_flag = subs_ordered 
                has_country_flag = toggle_adio
            }
		}
        
        complete_effect = {
            set_country_flag = subs_ordered
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_favor_boost_mediocre_from_tt
        }
        remove_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = { original_tag = GER }
                } 
                create_equipment_variant = {
                    name = "U-boat Class"
                    type = ship_hull_submarine_3
                    name_group = GRE_SS_HISTORICAL
                    parent_version = 0
                    modules = {
                        fixed_ship_torpedo_slot = ship_torpedo_sub_3
                        mid_1_custom_slot = ship_sub_snorkel_1
                        fixed_ship_engine_slot = sub_ship_engine_3
                        rear_1_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_sub_3
                    }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = {
                        GER = { NOT = { has_war_with = ENG } }
                    }              
                    resize_array = { ship_builder = 12 }                ## Tell it to build 12 ships
                }
                else = {
                    resize_array = { ship_builder = 6 }                 ## Tell it to build  6 ships
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = { original_tag = ENG }
                } 
                create_equipment_variant = {
                    name = "Undine Class"
                    type = ship_hull_submarine_3
                    name_group = GRE_SS_HISTORICAL
                    parent_version = 0
                    modules = {
                        fixed_ship_torpedo_slot = ship_torpedo_sub_3
                        mid_1_custom_slot = ship_sub_snorkel_1
                        fixed_ship_engine_slot = sub_ship_engine_3
                        rear_1_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_sub_3
                    }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = {
                        GER = { NOT = { has_war_with = ENG } }
                    }
                    resize_array = { ship_builder = 12 }                ## Tell it to build 12 ships
                }
                else = {
                    resize_array = { ship_builder = 6 }                 ## Tell it to build  6 ships
                }
            }
            spawn_subs = yes                                            ### -> Scripted effect
        }
    }

            }

        }
    }

GRE_pay_back_debt_to_the_ifc_category = { 

    GRE_pay_debt_small = {
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { state = FROM.capital }                 ### CHECK IF BOTH FAVOR AND THIS WORK PROPERLY AS THEY BOTH TARGET CAPITAL (IF BOTH SHOW)

		icon = hol_attract_foreign_investors

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
            NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                OR = {
                    original_tag = ENG
                    original_tag = FRA
                    original_tag = ITA 
                }
			}
		}

		cost = 10
        days_remove = 1

		fire_only_once = no

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRE_reevaluating_the_drachma
			has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_debt_to_the_ifc_dyn }
			NOT = {   
				OR = {
					check_variable = { GRE.debt@FROM = 0 }
                    has_country_flag = GRE_small_installment_payment_flag
                    has_country_flag = GRE_large_installment_payment_flag
				}
			}
		}
        
        complete_effect = {
            add_ideas = GRE_paying_off_debt_small
			hidden_effect = { 
				set_country_flag = { flag = GRE_small_installment_payment_flag value = 1 days = 1 }
			}
        }

		remove_effect = {
            FROM = { add_political_power = 10 }
            set_variable = { GRE.debt_package = 5 }
            FROM = { GRE_update_debt_status = yes }
            remove_ideas = GRE_paying_off_debt_small
		}    
    }

		icon = hol_attract_foreign_investors

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
        
        visible = {
            OR = {
                has_idea = GRE_arms_deal

                has_idea = GRE_arms_deal_2
            }

            NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_debt_free }
        }

        cost = 0

					remove_idea = GRE_arms_deal
					add_idea = GRE_arms_deal_1
				}
            }
            else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GRE_arms_deal_1
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GRE_arms_deal_1
					add_idea = GRE_arms_deal_2
				}
            }
            else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GRE_arms_deal_2
				}
                remove_ideas = GRE_arms_deal_2
            }
            set_country_flag = GRE_extra_gold_for_debt
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_utilize_gold_reserves_for_further_debt_repayment_tt
            set_variable = { GRE_debt_tokens = 3 }
		}
	}

            custom_effect_tooltip = "We will have a moderate influence increase with the British."       
            add_to_variable = { ENG.favor@GRE = 6 }
            ENG = {
                random_owned_controlled_state = {
                    add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
                    add_building_construction = {
                        type = synthetic_refinery
                        level = 3
                        instant_build = yes
                    }
                }            
            }
            random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 186 }
               	limit = {
                    free_building_slots = {
                       	building = synthetic_refinery
                        size > 0
                        include_locked = yes
                    }
                }
                add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
                add_building_construction = {
                    type = synthetic_refinery
                    level = 2
                    instant_build = yes
                }
            }
            set_variable = { GRE_lignite_partner = ENG.id }
        }
    }

#Greece Hellenic Academy decisions
GRE_hellenic_academy_category = {
	GRE_reform_the_army = {
		icon = ges

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var = GRE_ges value = 2 compare = less_than }
                }
                OR = {
                    has_army_experience > 74.99
                    has_completed_focus = GRE_conduct_exercises
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {            
                    check_variable = { var = GRE_ges value = 2 compare = equals }    
                }
                has_army_experience > 149.99
                has_country_flag = GRE_victor_in_a_war   
                NOT = { has_idea = GRE_army_leadership_0 } 	        
            }  
            else_if = {
                limit = {            
                    check_variable = { var = GRE_ges value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                }
                has_army_experience > 199.99
                has_country_flag = GRE_victor_in_a_big_war   
                NOT = { has_idea = GRE_army_leadership_0 } 	
                NOT = { has_idea = GRE_airforce_leadership_0 }                    
            }            
        }

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
        
        visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_hellenic_armed_forces
            NOT = { check_variable = { var = GRE_ges value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
        }

		fire_only_once = no

        days_remove = 90
            
		remove_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = { has_completed_focus = GRE_conduct_exercises }
                    check_variable = { var = GRE_ges value = 2 compare = less_than }
                }
               army_experience = -75
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    has_completed_focus = GRE_conduct_exercises 
                    check_variable = { var = GRE_ges value = 2 compare = less_than }
                }
                army_experience = 5
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var = GRE_ges value = 2 compare = equals }
                }
                army_experience = -150
            }
            else = {
                army_experience = -200
            }
            GRE_army_reform_tr = yes
            add_to_variable = { GRE_ges = 1 } 
		}
	}

		cost = 0

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_dlc = "Man the Guns" }
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = battleship_1
					}
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.8
					amount = 1
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = battleship_1
					}
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.75
					amount = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
				hidden_effect = { 
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Mississippi Class"
						type = ship_hull_heavy_1
						name_group = GRE_BB_HISTORICAL
						parent_version = 0
						modules = { 
							fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_heavy_battery_2
							fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_1 
							fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_0
							fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
							fixed_ship_engine_slot = heavy_ship_engine_1 
							fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = ship_secondaries_1
							fixed_ship_armor_slot = ship_armor_bb_2 
							front_1_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_1
							front_2_custom_slot = empty 
							mid_1_custom_slot = ship_secondaries_1 
							mid_2_custom_slot = empty
							mid_3_custom_slot = empty 
							rear_1_custom_slot = ship_heavy_battery_1 
							rear_2_custom_slot = empty 
						} 
					}	
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ship_hull_heavy_1
						creator = "GRE" 
						version_name = "Mississippi Class"
					}
					name = "Kilkis" 
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.8
					amount = 1
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ship_hull_heavy_1
						creator = "GRE" 
						version_name = "Mississippi Class"
					}
					name = "Lemnos" 
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.6
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_naval_factories > 12
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}

GRE_the_resource_storage_plan = {

    the_resource_plan_oil = { 
		icon = generic_operation

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_spend_gold_for_resources
            check_variable = { var = GRE_resource_choices value = 1 compare = less_than_or_equals }
            num_of_civilian_factories > 4
		}

		visible = {
            #NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_getting_resources }
            has_completed_focus = GRE_spend_gold_for_resources
            check_variable = { var = GRE_resource_choices value = 1 compare = less_than_or_equals }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 120
        
        modifier = {
            civilian_factory_use = 5
        }
        
        complete_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { GRE_resource_choices = 1 }
            set_country_flag = GRE_getting_resources
        }
        
        remove_effect = {
            set_country_flag = GRE_res_plan_oil_secured  
            clr_country_flag = GRE_getting_resources
        }
    }

    unearth_the_hidden_resources_oil = {
		icon = generic_operation

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
            OR = {
                has_country_flag = GRE_res_plan_oil_secured
                has_country_flag = GRE_res_plan_oil_secured_2
                }
		}

		visible = {
                OR = {
                has_country_flag = GRE_res_plan_oil_secured
                has_country_flag = GRE_res_plan_oil_secured_2
                }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
        
        days_remove = 120
        
        complete_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                has_country_flag = GRE_res_plan_oil_secured_2
                }
                186 = { 
                    add_resource = { 
                        type = oil
                        amount = 40
                    }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                has_country_flag = GRE_res_plan_oil_secured
                }
                186 = { 
                    add_resource = { 
                        type = oil
                        amount = 20
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        remove_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                has_country_flag = GRE_res_plan_oil_secured_2
                }
                186 = { 
                    add_resource = { 
                        type = oil
                        amount = -40
                    }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                has_country_flag = GRE_res_plan_oil_secured
                }
                186 = { 
                    add_resource = { 
                        type = oil
                        amount = -20
                    }
                }
            }
        }

GRE_economic_fluidity = {

    GRE_expand_collapse_tariff_decisions = {
        icon = decision_generic_decision
    
        allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}
        
        fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 0
        days_re_enable = 0
        priority = 12
        
        visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_tariff
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
        }
        
        complete_effect = {
            hidden_effect = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_tariff }
                    }
                    set_country_flag = toggle_tariff
                }
                else = {
                    clr_country_flag = toggle_tariff
                }
            }
        }
    }

    impose_tarrifs = {
    
		icon = tariff

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                is_in_array = {
                    array = global.favor_mechanic
                    value = THIS.id
                }          
			}
		}
        
        available = {
            has_country_flag = GRE_debt_free
        }
        
        available = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_open_foreign_subsidized_factories
            has_completed_focus = GRE_bedrock_of_balkan_financial_stability
            has_completed_focus = GRE_economic_fluidity_plans
        }
        
        visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_tariff
            if = {
                limit = {
                    FROM = { is_major = no }
                }
                check_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE > 49 }
            }
            FROM = { NOT = { has_idea = GRtar_trade_3 } }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = toggle_tariff }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_government_in_exile }
        }

        cost = 50

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 0

		complete_effect = {
            FROM = { 
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_idea = GRtar_trade_2
                    }
                    swap_ideas = {
                        remove_idea = GRtar_trade_2
                        add_idea = GRtar_trade_3
                    }
                    set_variable = { GRE.tariff_level@FROM = 3 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_idea = GRtar_trade_1
                    }
                    swap_ideas = {
                        remove_idea = GRtar_trade_1
                        add_idea = GRtar_trade_2
                    }
                    set_variable = { GRE.tariff_level@FROM = 2 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_ideas = GRtar_trade_1
                    set_variable = { GRE.tariff_level@FROM = 1 }
                }
            }
		}    
    }
    
    reduce_tariffs = {

            if = {
                limit = {

    army_buffs = {
		icon = generic_operation

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
            date > 1939.1.1
		}

		visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_army_reborn
            check_variable = { var = GRE_army_reform_cnt value = 10 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 1

        
        complete_effect = {
            set_country_flag = GRE_metaxas_army_mobilized
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_army_buffs_tt
            add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_army_reform_hellenic_staff }
            add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_army_reform_hellenic_army }
            #add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_army_reform_hellenic_people }         (THIS WILL BE ADDED BY THE PEOPLE'S SACRIFICE)   
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var = GRE_army_reform_cnt value = 15 compare = less_than_or_equals }
                    has_idea = GRE_army_status_0
                }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GRE_army_status_0
					add_idea = GRE_army_status_1
				}
                set_variable = { GRE_ges = 1 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var = GRE_army_reform_cnt value = 15 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                    has_idea = GRE_army_status_0
                }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GRE_army_status_0
					add_idea = GRE_army_status_2
				}
                set_variable = { GRE_ges = 2 }
            }
            else_if {
                limit = {
                    has_idea = GRE_army_status_1
                }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GRE_army_status_1
					add_idea = GRE_army_status_2
				}
                set_variable = { GRE_ges = 2 }   
            }
        }
    }

    ### ITALIAN PATH ###
    
    approach_the_italians = {
		icon = generic_operation
        priority = 2

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_the_italian_question
            has_completed_focus = GRE_rapprochement_with_the_italians
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = GRE_debt_free_italian_tt
                check_variable = { GRE_debt_to_the_ifc_italy_var = 0 compare = less_than_or_equals }
            }
		}

		visible = {
            has_completed_focus = GRE_the_italian_question
            NOT = { has_war_with = ITA }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_italians_responded }
            ITA = { has_government = fascism }
            GER = { has_government = fascism }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 90

        cost = 75
        fixed_random_seed = no
        
        remove_effect = {               ### THE FOLLOWING CALCULATES THE FAVOR OF BOTH ITALY AND THE GERMANS (weighted 80% for italians, 20% for germans) and slowly drags the readiness variable towards 100, where italians will accept rapproachment###
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { GRE_italian_readiness = 100 compare = less_than_or_equals }
                }
                random_list = {
                    85 = {
                        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_italian_rapproachment_85_tt
                        set_temp_variable = { x = ITA.favor@GRE }
                        set_temp_variable = { y = GER.favor@GRE }
                        clamp_temp_variable = {
                            var = x
                            min = 0
                            max = 100                       
                        }
                        clamp_temp_variable = {
                            var = y
                            min = 0
                            max = 100                       
                        }                        
                        multiply_temp_variable = { x = 0.8 }
                        multiply_temp_variable = { y = 0.2 } 
                        add_to_temp_variable = { x = y }
                        multiply_temp_variable = { x = 0.5 } 
                        add_to_variable = { GRE_italian_readiness = x }
                    }
                    10 = {
                        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_italian_rapproachment_10_tt
                        subtract_from_variable = { GRE_italian_readiness = 5 }
                    }
                    5 = {
                        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_italian_rapproachment_5_tt
                        set_country_flag = GRE_italians_responded
                        hidden_effect = {
                            country_event = { id = hellas.323 days = 0 }  
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            else = {
                set_country_flag = GRE_italians_responded
                country_event = { id = hellas.323 days = 0 }
            }
        }
    }

GRE_infl_majors_category = {

    GRE_win_major_favor = {
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { state = FROM.capital }

		icon = deal

		allowed = { 
			tag = GRE
		}

		available = {
            FROM = { has_opinion = { target = GRE value > 0 } }
            NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
                OR = {
                    original_tag = USA
                    original_tag = ENG 
                    original_tag = FRA 
                    original_tag = SOV 
                    original_tag = GER
                    original_tag = JAP
                    original_tag = ITA
                }
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		fire_only_once = no

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRE_a_game_of_shadows
		}

		remove_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 10 }
            add_to_variable = { GRE_total_favor = 10 }
		}    
    }
}

GRE_government_in_exile_category = {

    GRE_swappero = {
    
        allowed = {
            original_tag = GRE
        }
    
        complete_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    event_target:hellenic_state = { is_ai = yes }
                }
                event_target:hellenic_state = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    GRE = { is_ai = yes }
                }
                GRE = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
            }
        }
    
    }

}
